3. Familiar with the common designing methods of game sound effects and music, and mastered the use of game audio middleware. Preferably with the capability of game audio sound designing and familiarity with the usage and mechanism of DAW.
4. Familiar with game engines such as Unity and Unreal or any other internal game engine. Have knowledge of the game development process. Mastering the method and integration mode of game audio, and having the experience and ability of game plug-in development.
5. Having a basic knowledge of digital signal analysis, familiar with Matlab/Python and other scripting languages. Familiar with the framework of common audio signal analysis and processing methods. Preferably with experience in related audio effector implementation.
6. Better to have knowledge of PD, MAX/MSP, FAUST, and other graphics audio programming languages, having the capability to quickly conduct audio synthesis and prototype design of audio effect.
7. Better to have knowledge of the mechanism of spatial acoustics technology, have the capability of spatial acoustics technology application and algorithm design, preferably with relevant development experience.
8. Better to have knowledge of basic music theory, have certain musical literacy, familiar with the related synthesis technology of music or musical instruments is preferred.
9. Strong teamwork ability, learning ability, and team spirit.
